## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-106">Sistemi operativi supportati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-106">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-107">Sono supportati i sistemi operativi seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-107">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-108">Windows 7 o versione successiva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-108">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 o versione successiva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-109">Windows Server 2012 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-110">Il [server HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (chiamato in precedenza WebListener) non funziona in una configurazione proxy inverso con IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-110">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-111">È necessario usare il [server Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-111">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-112">Per informazioni sull'hosting in Azure, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-112">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-113">Per linee guida per la risoluzione dei problemi, vedere <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-113">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-114">Piattaforme supportate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-114">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-115">Sono supportate le app pubblicate per la distribuzione a 32 bit (x86) o a 64 bit (x64).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-115">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-116">Distribuire un'app a 32 bit con .NET Core SDK a 32 bit (x86), a meno che l'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-116">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-117">Non richieda lo spazio indirizzi di memoria virtuale più grande disponibile per un'app a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-117">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-118">Non richieda le dimensioni maggiori dello stack IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-118">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-119">Non abbia dipendenze native a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-119">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-120">Usare .NET Core SDK a 64 bit (x64) per pubblicare un'app a 64 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-120">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-121">Un runtime a 64 bit deve essere presente nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-121">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

## <a name="hosting-models"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-122">Modelli di hosting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-122">Hosting models</span></span>

### <a name="in-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-123">Modello di hosting in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-123">In-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-124">Se si usa l'hosting in-process, un'app ASP.NET Core esegue lo stesso processo del processo di lavoro IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-124">Using in-process hosting, an ASP.NET Core app runs in the same process as its IIS worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-125">L'hosting in-process offre prestazioni migliori rispetto all'hosting out-of-process perché le richieste non vengono inserite in proxy sulla scheda di loopback, un'interfaccia di rete che restituisce il traffico di rete in uscita allo stesso computer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-125">In-process hosting provides improved performance over out-of-process hosting because requests aren't proxied over the loopback adapter, a network interface that returns outgoing network traffic back to the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-126">Per gestire il processo, IIS usa il [servizio Attivazione processo Windows (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-126">IIS handles process management with the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-127">Il [modulo principale ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-127">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-128">Esegue l'inizializzazione dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-128">Performs app initialization.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-129">Carica [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-129">Loads the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-130">Chiama `Program.Main`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-130">Calls `Program.Main`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3e595-131">Gestisce la durata della richiesta nativa di IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-131">Handles the lifetime of the IIS native request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-132">Il modello di hosting In-Process non è supportato per le app ASP.NET Core destinate a .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-132">The in-process hosting model isn't supported for ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-133">Il diagramma seguente illustra la relazione tra IIS, il modulo ASP.NET Core e un'app ospitata in-process:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-133">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted in-process:</span></span>

![Modulo ASP.NET Core nello scenario di hosting in-process](index/_static/ancm-inprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-135">Una richiesta arriva dal Web al driver HTTP.sys in modalità kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-135">A request arrives from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-136">Il driver instrada la richiesta nativa IIS sulla porta configurata per il sito Web, in genere 80 (HTTP) o 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-136">The driver routes the native request to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-137">Il modulo di base ASP.NET riceve la richiesta nativa`IISHttpServer`e la passa al server HTTP IIS ( ).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-137">The ASP.NET Core Module receives the native request and passes it to IIS HTTP Server (`IISHttpServer`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-138">Il server HTTP di IIS è un'implementazione di server in-process per IIS che converte la richiesta da nativa a gestita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-138">IIS HTTP Server is an in-process server implementation for IIS that converts the request from native to managed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-139">Dopo che la richiesta è stata elaborata dal server HTTP di IIS, viene eseguito il push della richiesta nella pipeline middleware ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-139">After the IIS HTTP Server processes the request, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-140">La pipeline middleware gestisce la richiesta e la passa come istanza di `HttpContext` alla logica dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-140">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-141">La risposta dell'app viene restituita a IIS tramite il server HTTP di IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-141">The app's response is passed back to IIS through IIS HTTP Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-142">IIS invia la risposta al client che ha avviato la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-142">IIS sends the response to the client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-143">L'hosting in-process è una funzionalità che richiede il consenso esplicito per le app esistenti, mentre i modelli [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) usano per impostazione predefinita il modello di hosting in-process per tutti gli scenari IIS e IIS Express.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-143">In-process hosting is opt-in for existing apps, but [dotnet new](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-new) templates default to the in-process hosting model for all IIS and IIS Express scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-144">`CreateDefaultBuilder` aggiunge un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> chiamando il metodo <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> per avviare [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) e ospitare l'app all'interno del processo di lavoro IIS (*w3wp.exe* o *iisexpress.exe*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-144">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adds an <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instance by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS*> method to boot the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) and host the app inside of the IIS worker process (*w3wp.exe* or *iisexpress.exe*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-145">I test delle prestazioni indicano che l'hosting di un'app .NET Core in-process offre una velocità effettiva delle richieste significativamente superiore rispetto all'hosting dell'app out-of-process o all'inoltro delle richieste al server [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-145">Performance tests indicate that hosting a .NET Core app in-process delivers significantly higher request throughput compared to hosting the app out-of-process and proxying requests to [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-146">Le app pubblicate come un singolo file eseguibile non possono essere caricate dal modello di hosting in-process.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-146">Apps published as a single file executable can't be loaded by the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

### <a name="out-of-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-147">Modello di hosting out-of-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-147">Out-of-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-148">Poiché le app ASP.NET Core vengono eseguite in un processo separato dal processo di lavoro IIS, il modulo di ASP.NET Core gestisce la gestione dei processi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-148">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the ASP.NET Core Module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-149">Il modulo avvia il processo per l'app ASP.NET Core quando arriva la prima richiesta e riavvia l'app se viene arrestata o si arresta in modo anomalo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-149">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-150">Si tratta essenzialmente dello stesso comportamento delle app eseguite in-process e gestite dal [servizio Attivazione processo Windows](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-150">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-151">Il diagramma seguente illustra la relazione tra IIS, il modulo ASP.NET Core e un'app ospitata out-of-process:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-151">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Modulo ASP.NET Core nello scenario di hosting out-of-process](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-153">Le richieste arrivano dal Web al driver HTTP.sys in modalità kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-153">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-154">Il driver instrada le richieste a IIS sulla porta configurata per il sito Web, in genere 80 (HTTP) o 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-154">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-155">Il modulo inoltra le richieste a Kestrel su una porta casuale per l'app non corrispondente alla porta 80 o 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-155">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-156">Il modulo specifica la porta tramite una variabile di ambiente all'avvio e l'estensione <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> configura il server per l'ascolto su `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-156">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> extension configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-157">Vengono eseguiti controlli aggiuntivi e le richieste che non provengono dal modulo vengono rifiutate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-157">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-158">Il modulo non supporta l'inoltro HTTPS, pertanto le richieste vengono inoltrate tramite HTTP anche se sono state ricevute da IIS tramite HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-158">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-159">Dopo che Kestrel ha prelevato la richiesta dal modulo, viene eseguito il push della richiesta nella pipeline middleware ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-159">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-160">La pipeline middleware gestisce la richiesta e la passa come istanza di `HttpContext` alla logica dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-160">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-161">Il middleware aggiunto dall'integrazione di IIS aggiorna lo schema, l'IP remoto e il percorso di base all'account per l'inoltro della richiesta a Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-161">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-162">La risposta dell'app viene quindi passata a IIS, che ne esegue di nuovo il push al client HTTP che ha avviato la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-162">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-163">Per indicazioni sulla configurazione del modulo ASP.NET Core, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-163">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-164">Per altre informazioni sull'hosting, vedere [Hosting in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-164">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-165">Configurazione dell'applicazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-165">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-166">Abilitare i componenti IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-166">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-167">Quando si compila `CreateHostBuilder` un host <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> in (*Program.cs*), chiamata per abilitare l'integrazione IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-167">When building a host in `CreateHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IHostBuilder CreateHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    Host.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-168">Per altre informazioni su `CreateDefaultBuilder`, vedere <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-168">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-169">Opzioni IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-169">IIS options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-170">**Modello di hosting in-process**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-170">**In-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-171">Per configurare le opzioni del server IIS includere una configurazione del servizio per <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-171">To configure IIS Server options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-172">L'esempio seguente disabilita AutomaticAuthentication:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-172">The following example disables AutomaticAuthentication:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISServerOptions>(options => 
{
    options.AutomaticAuthentication = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="3e595-173">Opzione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-173">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-174">Predefinito</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-174">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-175">Impostazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-175">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-176">Se `true`, IIS Server imposta l'utente `HttpContext.User` autenticato tramite l'[autenticazione di Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-176">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-177">Se `false`, il server fornisce solo un'identità per `HttpContext.User` e risponde alle richieste esplicite di `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-177">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-178">Per il funzionamento di `AutomaticAuthentication` l’autenticazione di Windows deve essere abilitata in IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-178">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-179">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Autenticazione di Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-179">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-180">Imposta il nome visualizzato dagli utenti nelle pagine di accesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-180">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `AllowSynchronousIO`           | `false` | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-181">Se l'I/O sincrono è consentito per il `HttpContext.Request` e il `HttpContext.Response`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-181">Whether synchronous I/O is allowed for the `HttpContext.Request` and the `HttpContext.Response`.</span></span> |
| `MaxRequestBodySize`           | `30000000`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-182">Ottiene o imposta la dimensione massima del corpo della richiesta per `HttpRequest`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-182">Gets or sets the max request body size for the `HttpRequest`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-183">Notare che IIS stesso include il limite `maxAllowedContentLength`, che verrà elaborato prima del set `MaxRequestBodySize` in `IISServerOptions`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-183">Note that IIS itself has the limit `maxAllowedContentLength` which will be processed before the `MaxRequestBodySize` set in the `IISServerOptions`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-184">La modifica di `MaxRequestBodySize` non influisce su `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-184">Changing the `MaxRequestBodySize` won't affect the `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-185">Per aumentare `maxAllowedContentLength`, aggiungere una voce in *web.config* per impostare `maxAllowedContentLength` su un valore superiore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-185">To increase `maxAllowedContentLength`, add an entry in the *web.config* to set `maxAllowedContentLength` to a higher value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-186">Per ulteriori informazioni, vedere [Configurazione](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-186">For more details, see [Configuration](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-187">**Modello di hosting out-of-process**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-187">**Out-of-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-188">Per configurare le opzioni di IIS includere una configurazione del servizio per <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-188">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-189">Nell'esempio seguente si impedisce all'app di popolare `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-189">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="3e595-190">Opzione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-190">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-191">Predefinito</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-191">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-192">Impostazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-192">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-193">Se `true`, il [middleware di integrazione IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) imposta `HttpContext.User` autenticato tramite l'[autenticazione di Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-193">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-194">Se `false`, il middleware fornisce solo un'identità per `HttpContext.User` e risponde solo alle richieste esplicite di `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-194">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-195">Per il funzionamento di `AutomaticAuthentication` l’autenticazione di Windows deve essere abilitata in IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-195">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-196">Per altre informazioni, vedere l'argomento [Autenticazione di Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-196">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-197">Imposta il nome visualizzato dagli utenti nelle pagine di accesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-197">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="3e595-198">Se è `true` ed è presente l’intestazione della richiesta `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT`, `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` viene popolato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-198">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-199">Scenari con server proxy e servizi di bilanciamento del carico</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-199">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-200">Il [middleware di integrazione IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), che consente di configurare il middleware delle intestazioni inoltrate, e il modulo ASP.NET Core sono configurati per inoltrare lo schema (HTTP/HTTPS) e l'indirizzo IP remoto di origine della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-200">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components), which configures Forwarded Headers Middleware, and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the scheme (HTTP/HTTPS) and the remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-201">Potrebbero essere necessari interventi di configurazione aggiuntivi per le app ospitate dietro ulteriori server proxy e servizi di bilanciamento del carico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-201">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-202">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Configurare ASP.NET Core per l'utilizzo di server proxy e servizi di bilanciamento del carico](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-202">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-203">File web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-203">web.config file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-204">Il file *web.config* configura il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-204">The *web.config* file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-205">La creazione, la trasformazione e la pubblicazione del file *web.config* sono operazioni gestite da una destinazione MSBuild (`_TransformWebConfig`) quando viene pubblicato il progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-205">Creating, transforming, and publishing the *web.config* file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-206">Questa destinazione si trova tra le destinazioni Web SDK (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-206">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-207">L'SDK è impostato all'inizio del file di progetto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-207">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-208">Se nel progetto non è presente un file *web.config*, il file viene creato con un valore *processPath* e *argomenti* corretti per la configurazione del modulo ASP.NET Core. Il file viene quindi spostato nell'[output pubblicato](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-208">If a *web.config* file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-209">Se nel progetto è presente un file *web.config*, il file viene trasformato con il valore di *processPath* e gli *argomenti* corretti per la configurazione del modulo ASP.NET Core, quindi viene spostato nell'output pubblicato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-209">If a *web.config* file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct *processPath* and *arguments* to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-210">La trasformazione non modifica le impostazioni di configurazione di IIS incluse nel file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-210">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-211">Il file *web.config* può fornire ulteriori impostazioni di configurazione di IIS che controllano i moduli IIS attivi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-211">The *web.config* file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-212">Per informazioni sui moduli IIS in grado di elaborare le richieste con le app di ASP.NET Core, vedere l'argomento [Moduli IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-212">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-213">Per impedire che Web SDK trasformi il file *web.config*, usare la proprietà **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled >** nel file di progetto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-213">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the *web.config* file, use the **\<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>** property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-214">Quando si disabilita la trasformazione del file in Web SDK, il valore di *processPath* e gli *argomenti* devono essere impostati manualmente dallo sviluppatore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-214">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the *processPath* and *arguments* should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-215">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-215">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-216">Posizione del file web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-216">web.config file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-217">Per configurare correttamente il [modulo di base di ASP.NET,](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) il file *web.config* deve essere presente nel percorso radice del [contenuto](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (in genere il percorso di base dell'app) dell'app distribuita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-217">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the *web.config* file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-218">Corrisponde al percorso fisico del sito Web fornito a IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-218">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-219">Il file *web.config* deve essere presente nella radice dell'app per abilitare la pubblicazione di più app mediante Distribuzione Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-219">The *web.config* file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-220">I file riservati sono presenti nel percorso fisico dell'app, ad \* \<esempio l'assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, \* \<l'assembly>.xml* (commenti relativi alla documentazione XML) e \* \<l'assembly>.deps.json\*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-220">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as *\<assembly>.runtimeconfig.json*, *\<assembly>.xml* (XML Documentation comments), and *\<assembly>.deps.json*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-221">Quando il file *web.config* è presente e il sito viene avviato normalmente, IIS non rende disponibili questi file riservati se vengono richiesti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-221">When the *web.config* file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-222">Se il file *web.config* non è presente, ha un nome non corretto o non è in grado di configurare il sito per l'avvio normale, IIS potrebbe rendere disponibili pubblicamente i file riservati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-222">If the *web.config* file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-223">**Il file *web.config* deve essere sempre presente nella distribuzione, denominato correttamente e in grado di configurare il sito per la normale avvio. Non rimuovere mai il file *web.config* da una distribuzione di produzione.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-223">**The *web.config* file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the *web.config* file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-224">Trasformare web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-224">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-225">Se è necessario trasformare *web.config* in fase di pubblicazione (ad esempio, impostare variabili di ambiente in base a configurazione, profilo o ambiente), vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-225">If you need to transform *web.config* on publish (for example, set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment), see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-226">Configurazione di IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-226">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-227">**Sistemi operativi Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-227">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-228">Abilitare il ruolo del server **Server Web (IIS)** e stabilire i servizi di ruolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-228">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-229">Usare la procedura guidata **Aggiungi ruoli e funzionalità** accessibile tramite il menu **Gestisci** o il collegamento in **Server Manager**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-229">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-230">Nel passaggio **Ruoli del server** selezionare la casella per **Server Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-230">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![Il ruolo Server Web IIS viene selezionato nel passaggio dei ruoli del server Selezionare.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-232">Dopo il passaggio **Funzionalità**, viene caricato il passaggio**Servizi ruolo** per Server Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-232">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-233">Selezionare i servizi ruolo IIS desiderati o accettare i servizi ruolo predefiniti specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-233">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![I servizi ruolo predefiniti vengono selezionati nel passaggio Selezionare i servizi ruolo.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-235">**Autenticazione di Windows (facoltativa)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-235">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-236">Per abilitare l'autenticazione di Windows, espandere i seguenti nodi: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-236">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-237">Selezionare la funzionalità **Autenticazione di Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-237">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-238">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Autenticazione di Windows\<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurare l'autenticazione Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-238">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-239">**WebSockets (facoltativo)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-239">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-240">WebSockets è supportato con ASP.NET Core 1.1 o versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-240">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-241">Per abilitare WebSockets, espandere i seguenti nodi:**Sviluppo di applicazioni**server >  **Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-241">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-242">Selezionare la funzionalità **Protocollo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-242">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-243">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Oggetti WebSocket](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-243">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-244">Procedere con il passaggio **Conferma** per installare il ruolo del server web e i servizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-244">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-245">Non è necessario riavviare server/IIS dopo l'installazione del ruolo **Server Web (IIS).**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-245">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-246">**Sistemi operativi desktop di Windows**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-246">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-247">Abilitare **Console di gestione IIS** e **Servizi Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-247">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-248">Passare a **Pannello di controllo** > **Programmi** > **Programmi e funzionalità** > **Disattivare o attivare le funzionalità di Windows** (a sinistra dello schermo).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-248">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-249">Aprire il nodo **Internet Information Services**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-249">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-250">Aprire il nodo **Strumenti di gestione Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-250">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-251">Selezionare la casella per **Console di gestione IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-251">Check the box for **IIS Management Console**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-252">Selezionare la casella per **Servizi World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-252">Check the box for **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-253">Accettare le funzionalità predefinite per **Servizi World Wide Web** o personalizzare le funzionalità IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-253">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-254">**Autenticazione di Windows (facoltativa)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-254">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-255">Per abilitare l'autenticazione di Windows, espandere i seguenti nodi: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-255">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-256">Selezionare la funzionalità **Autenticazione di Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-256">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-257">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Autenticazione di Windows\<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurare l'autenticazione Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-257">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-258">**WebSockets (facoltativo)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-258">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-259">WebSockets è supportato con ASP.NET Core 1.1 o versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-259">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-260">Per abilitare WebSockets, espandere i nodi seguenti: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-260">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-261">Selezionare la funzionalità **Protocollo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-261">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-262">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Oggetti WebSocket](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-262">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-263">Se l'installazione di IIS richiede un riavvio, riavviare il sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-263">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

![La console di gestione IIS e servizi World Wide Web sono selezionati nelle funzionalità di Windows.](index/_static/windows-features-win10.png)

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-265">Installare il bundle di hosting .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-265">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-269">Se il bundle di hosting viene installato prima di IIS, è necessario riparare l'installazione del bundle.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-269">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-270">Eseguire di nuovo il programma di installazione del bundle di hosting dopo l'installazione di IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-270">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-271">Se il bundle di hosting viene installato dopo l'installazione della versione a 64 bit (x64) di .NET Core, uno o più SDK potrebbero risultare mancanti ([Non sono stati rilevati .NET Core SDK](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-271">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-272">Per risolvere il problema, vedere <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-272">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-284">Installare il bundle di hosting</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-284">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-285">Eseguire il programma di installazione nel server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-285">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-286">Quando si esegue il programma di installazione da una shell dei comandi di amministratore sono disponibili i parametri seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-286">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-287">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`&ndash; Saltare l'installazione del ASP.NET Core Module.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-287">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-288">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`&ndash; Ignorare l'installazione del runtime di .NET Core.Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-288">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1` &ndash; Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-289">Utilizzato quando il server ospita solo [distribuzioni autonome (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-289">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-290">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`&ndash; Ignorare l'installazione di ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-290">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-291">Utilizzato quando il server ospita solo [distribuzioni autonome (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-291">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-292">`OPT_NO_X86=1`&ndash; Saltare l'installazione di runtime x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-292">`OPT_NO_X86=1` &ndash; Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-293">Usare questo parametro se si è certi che non verrà eseguito l'hosting di app a 32 bit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-293">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-294">Se non esiste alcuna possibilità che in futuro venga eseguito l'hosting di app sia a 32 che a 64 bit, non usare questo parametro e installare entrambi i runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-294">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="3e595-295">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Disabilitare il controllo dell'uso di una configurazione condivisa di IIS quando la configurazione condivisa (*applicationHost.config*) è nello stesso computer dell'installazione di IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-295">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-296">*Disponibile solo per i programmi di installazione di bundler di hosting ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-296">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-297">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-297">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-298">Riavviare il sistema o eseguire i seguenti comandi in una shell dei comandi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-298">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-299">Il riavvio di IIS rileva una modifica alla variabile di ambiente di sistema PATH apportata dal programma di installazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-299">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-300">ASP.NET Core non adotta il comportamento di rollforward per le versioni delle patch dei pacchetti framework condivisi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-300">ASP.NET Core doesn't adopt roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-301">Dopo aver aggiornato il framework condiviso installando un nuovo pacchetto di hosting, riavviare il sistema o eseguire i comandi seguenti in una shell dei comandi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-301">After upgrading the shared framework by installing a new hosting bundle, restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

```console
net stop was /y
net start w3svc
```

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-302">Per informazioni sulla configurazione condivisa di IIS, vedere [Modulo di ASP.NET Core con configurazione condivisa di IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-302">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-303">Installare la Distribuzione Web quando si pubblica con Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-303">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-304">Quando si distribuiscono app ai server con [Distribuzione Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), installare la versione più recente di Distribuzione Web nel server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-304">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-305">Per installare Distribuzione Web usare l'[Installazione guidata piattaforma Web (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) o ottenere direttamente un programma di installazione in [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-305">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-306">Il metodo preferito consiste nell'usare WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-306">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-307">WebPI offre un'installazione autonoma e una configurazione per i provider di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-307">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-308">Creare il sito IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-308">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-309">Nel sistema host creare una cartella per contenere le cartelle e i file pubblicati dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-309">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-310">In un passaggio successivo, il percorso della cartella viene fornito a IIS come percorso fisico dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-310">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-311">Per altre informazioni sulla cartella di distribuzione e il layout dei file di un'app, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-311">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-312">In Gestione IIS, aprire il nodo del server nel pannello **Connessioni.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-312">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-313">Fare clic con il pulsante destro del mouse sulla cartella **Siti**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-313">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-314">Scegliere **Aggiungi sito Web** dal menu di scelta rapida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-314">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-315">Specificare un **Nome del sito** e impostare il **Percorso fisico** per la cartella di distribuzione dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-315">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-316">Specificare la configurazione **Binding** e creare il sito Web selezionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-316">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Specificare il nome del sito, il percorso fisico e il nome Host nel passaggio Aggiungi sito Web.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="3e595-318">Le associazioni con caratteri jolly di livello superiore (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **non** devono essere usate,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-318">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-319">poiché possono introdurre vulnerabilità a livello di sicurezza nell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-319">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-320">Questo concetto vale sia per i caratteri jolly sicuri che vulnerabili.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-320">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-321">Usare nomi host espliciti al posto di caratteri jolly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-321">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-322">L'associazione con caratteri jolly del sottodominio (ad esempio, `*.mysub.com`) non costituisce un rischio per la sicurezza se viene controllato l'intero dominio padre (a differenza di `*.com`, che è vulnerabile).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-322">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-323">Vedere la [sezione 5.4 di RFC7230](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) per altre informazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-323">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-324">Nel nodo del server selezionare **Pool di applicazioni**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-324">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-325">Fare clic con il pulsante destro del mouse sul pool di applicazioni del sito e scegliere **Impostazioni di base** dal menu di scelta rapida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-325">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-326">Nella finestra **Modifica pool di applicazioni** impostare **Versione .NET CLR** su **Nessun codice gestito**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-326">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Impostare Nessun codice gestito per la versione .NET CLR.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="3e595-328">ASP.NET Core viene eseguito in un processo separato e gestisce il runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-328">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-329">ASP.NET Core non si basa sul caricamento di Common Language Runtime (CLR di .NET) desktop. Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core viene avviato per ospitare l'app nel processo di lavoro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-329">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-330">L'impostazione di **Versione .NET CLR** su **Nessun codice gestito** è facoltativa ma consigliata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-330">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-331">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive*: per una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) a 64 bit (x64) che usa il [modello di hosting In-Process](#in-process-hosting-model), disabilitare il pool di app per i processi a 32 bit (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-331">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-332">Nella barra laterale **Azioni** in Gestione IIS > **Pool di applicazioni** selezionare **Impostazioni predefinite pool di applicazioni** o **Impostazioni avanzate**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-332">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-333">Individuare **Attiva applicazioni a 32 bit** e impostare il valore su `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-333">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-334">Questa impostazione non viene applicata alle app distribuite per l'[hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-334">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3e595-335">Confermare che l'identità del modello del processo disponga delle autorizzazioni appropriate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-335">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="3e595-336">Se l'identità predefinita del pool di applicazioni (**Identità\*\*\*\*modello** > di processo ) viene modificata da **ApplicationPoolIdentity** a un'altra identità, verificare che la nuova identità disponga delle autorizzazioni necessarie per accedere alla cartella, al database e ad altre risorse necessarie dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-336">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-337">Ad esempio, il pool di applicazioni richiede l'accesso in lettura e scrittura alle cartelle in cui l'app legge e scrive i file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-337">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-338">**Configurazione dell'autenticazione di Windows (facoltativa)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-338">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="3e595-339">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Configurare l'autenticazione Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-339">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-340">Distribuire l'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-340">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-341">Distribuire l'app nella cartella **Percorso fisico** di IIS specificata nella sezione [Creare il sito IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-341">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-342">[Distribuzione Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) è il meccanismo consigliato per la distribuzione, ma esistono diverse opzioni per spostare l'app dalla cartella di *pubblicazione* del progetto alla cartella di distribuzione del sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-342">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-343">Distribuzione web con Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-343">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-344">Vedere l'argomento [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) (Profili di pubblicazione Visual Studio per la distribuzione di app ASP.NET Core) per informazioni su come creare un profilo di pubblicazione da usare con Distribuzione Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-344">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-345">Se il provider di hosting fornisce un profilo di pubblicazione o il supporto per crearne uno, scaricare il profilo e importarlo usando la finestra di dialogo **Pubblica** di Visual Studio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-345">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-347">Distribuzione Web all'esterno di Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-347">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-348">È anche possibile usare [Distribuzione Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) all'esterno di Visual Studio dalla riga di comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-348">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3e595-349">Per altre informazioni sulla distribuzione, vedere [Strumento Distribuzione Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-349">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-350">Alternative a Distribuzione web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-350">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3e595-351">Usare uno dei metodi disponibili, ad esempio la copia manuale, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) o [PowerShell](/powershell/), per spostare l'app nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-351">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="3e595-353">Esplorare il sito Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3e595-353">Browse the website</span></span>
